  ) -> None:\n   451→        \"\"\"Parse a module and recursively follow its imports.\"\"\"\n   452→        if module_name in self._parsed_modules:\n   453→            return\n   454→        if depth _extract_module(self, fqn: str, source_root: Path) -> str | None:\n   490→        \"\"\"Try progressively shorter prefixes of a FQN to find a module on disk.\"\"\"\n   491→        parts =
